Notice: `_bd_prev_page=https://teznevisan7.com/` â†’ **Your old domain** is the referrer![^20_1][^20_2][^20_3]

## ğŸš¨ The 403 Problem

**Why 403 is BAD for SEO:**

- 403 (Forbidden) tells Google "this page exists but you can't access it"
- Google will **eventually deindex** these pages, but slowly
- Better to use **404 (Not Found)** or **410 (Gone)** for faster removal[^20_2][^20_1]


## âœ… What You Did RIGHT

Your GSC removals are **good**, but **incomplete**:


| Pattern | Status | Assessment |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| `?gl=` | âœ“ Removed | Google Analytics parameter |
| `?h=` | âœ“ Removed | Hash/tracking parameter |
| `?route=` | âœ“ Removed | E-commerce spam |
| `?msclkid=` | âœ“ Removed | Bing Ads tracking |
| `?gclid=` | âœ“ Removed | Google Ads tracking |
| `?fbclid=` | âœ“ Removed | Facebook tracking |
| `?_bd_prev_page=` | âœ“ Removed | Baidu tracking (Chinese spam) |
| `?_bdsid=` | âœ“ Removed | Baidu session ID |
| `?_gid=` | âœ“ Removed | Google Analytics ID |

## âŒ What's MISSING from Your Removals

Based on Grok's analysis and the URL you showed, add these:

```
?e=                  (dominant spam pattern - ~50% of spam URLs)
?channel=            (affiliate spam)
?from=               (referral spam, e.g., from=blog.php)
?_ga=                (Google Analytics - complements _gid)
?_gcl_au=            (Google Ads conversion)
/page/*?             (paginated spam with parameters)
/public/themes/      (exposed theme files)
```


## ğŸ› ï¸ Complete Fix Strategy

### **Step 1: Fix 403 â†’ 404/410 (Add to .htaccess)**

Add this to your `.htaccess` file **right after** the security rules we added earlier:

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SPAM URL PARAMETER HANDLING - Return 410 Gone
# ============================================================================

# Block common tracking/spam parameters with 410 (faster deindex than 404)
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)(_gl|_gid|_ga|_gcl_au|_bdsid|_bd_prev_page)= [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)(gclid|fbclid|msclkid|utm_|ref=|referrer=)= [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)(e|h|channel|from|route)= [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block spam pagination patterns
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/page/[0-9]+/$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} !^$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block exposed theme files from indexing
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/public/themes/ [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/wp-content/themes/.*/css/ [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/wp-content/themes/.*/js/ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [F,L]

# Block Japanese/Chinese encoded spam
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} %E3%82%B3%E3%83%A2%E3%83%AA [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} %E3%83% [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]
```


### **Step 2: Add Missing GSC Removals (Do This NOW)**

Go to **Google Search Console** â†’ **Removals** â†’ **Temporary removals** â†’ **New request**:

Add these patterns (select "Remove all URLs with this prefix"):

```
https://teznevisan3.com/?e=
https://teznevisan3.com/?channel=
https://teznevisan3.com/?from=
https://teznevisan3.com/?_ga=
https://teznevisan3.com/?_gcl_au=
https://teznevisan3.com/page/2/?
https://teznevisan3.com/page/3/?
https://teznevisan3.com/page/4/?
https://teznevisan3.com/page/5/?
https://teznevisan3.com/public/themes/
https://www.teznevisan3.com/?e=
https://www.teznevisan3.com/?channel=
https://www.teznevisan3.com/?from=
```

**Important:** Also add the **www** versions if your site has both.

### **Step 3: Update robots.txt**

Add these disallow rules to `/robots.txt`:

```
User-agent: *
# Block spam parameters
Disallow: /*?e=*
Disallow: /*?channel=*
Disallow: /*?from=*
Disallow: /*?_gl=*
Disallow: /*?_gid=*
Disallow: /*?_ga=*
Disallow: /*?gclid=*
Disallow: /*?fbclid=*
Disallow: /*?msclkid=*
Disallow: /*?h=*
Disallow: /*?route=*
Disallow: /*?_bd*

# Block exposed theme files
Disallow: /public/themes/
Disallow: /wp-content/themes/*/css/
Disallow: /wp-content/themes/*/js/

# Block paginated spam
Disallow: /page/*?*
```


### **Step 4: Fix "Crawled - Currently Not Indexed"**

For the **legitimate pages** showing this status (like `/writing-thesis`, `/extracting-paper-from-dissertation/`):

1. **Request Indexing in GSC:**
    - Go to URL Inspection tool
    - Enter each good URL
    - Click "Request Indexing"
    - Do this for your top 10-20 important pages
2. **Improve Content Quality:**
    - Make sure these pages have 800+ words
    - Add unique, valuable content
    - Include relevant images with alt text
    - Add internal links to/from other pages
3. **Update Sitemap:**
    - Remove ALL spam URLs from your XML sitemap
    - Only include legitimate pages
    - Resubmit in GSC

### **Step 5: Handle Old Domain Spam Source**

Since we're **disavowing your old domains** (teznevisan7.com, etc.), you need to:

1. **Remove 301 redirects** from old domains (if you haven't yet)
2. **Remove "Change of Address"** in GSC for old domains
3. This will stop new spam from flowing through

### **Step 6: Monitor \& Clean**

**Week 1-2 Actions:**

```
â–¡ Check GSC daily for new spam URLs
â–¡ Run WordFence scan weekly
â–¡ Monitor 404 log for new patterns
â–¡ Update .htaccess if new spam appears
```

**After 2 Weeks:**

```
â–¡ Re-run GSC Pages report
â–¡ Verify "Crawled - not indexed" count dropped
â–¡ Request indexing for good pages that recovered
â–¡ Remove temporary GSC removals (they expire after 6 months)
```

## ğŸ¯ The Problem

Your **403 errors** (like `https://teznevisan3.com/page/5/?_gl=...`) are **BAD for SEO** because:

- Google sees "access denied" but keeps trying to crawl
- **410 (Gone)** is 50-70% faster for deindexing than 403
- 410 tells Google "permanently deleted, stop checking"[^21_1][^21_2][^21_3]

# This link:

[https://teznevisan3.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=rest-nonce](https://teznevisan3.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=rest-nonce)

Opens and shows this: bb4971cb65

This is just one that is on search console but there might be more, shouldn't we block access to themes and plugin files and other critical wordpress files?

**STOP! Don't block that endpoint** - it's actually **required** for WordPress to function properly. Let me explain what's happening and what's actually safe vs. what needs securing.

## ğŸ” What You're Seeing (It's Normal)

The URL `https://teznevisan3.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=rest-nonce` showing `bb4971cb65` is:

âœ… **SAFE and NORMAL** - This is a WordPress REST API nonce endpoint
âœ… **REQUIRED** - Many plugins and WordPress features need this to work
âœ… **NOT a security risk** - The nonce (bb4971cb65) is:

- User-session specific (unique per visitor)
- Rotated every 12-24 hours automatically
- Useless without valid authentication cookies

**DO NOT BLOCK THIS** or you'll break:

- WordPress admin functionality
- Plugin AJAX requests
- Contact forms
- WooCommerce (if you add it)
- Many theme features


## âš ï¸ Your Current Security (Already Good)

Looking at your existing setup from earlier, you **already have**:

### In robots.txt:

```
Disallow: /wp-admin/
Allow: /wp-admin/admin-ajax.php  â† Correctly allowed!
```


### In .htaccess (Section 6):

You already have protection against suspicious query strings but correctly exclude legitimate WordPress functionality.

### WordFence:

Already installed and protecting wp-admin with 2FA.

## âœ… What You SHOULD Block (Already Covered)

Here's what's **already blocked** in your current setup:


| File/Directory | Status | Reason |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| `/wp-admin/` | âœ… Blocked in robots.txt (except admin-ajax.php) | Prevents crawling admin pages |
| `/wp-config.php` | âœ… Blocked in .htaccess | Critical config file |
| `/wp-includes/` | âœ… Blocked in robots.txt | WordPress core files |
| `/xmlrpc.php` | âœ… Blocked in robots.txt | Common attack vector |
| `readme.html` | âœ… Blocked in robots.txt | Version disclosure |
| PHP in `/uploads/` | âœ… Blocked in .htaccess | Prevents malicious uploads |

## ğŸ›¡ï¸ Additional Hardening (Recommended)

Add these to your **.htaccess Section 3B** (after the spam blocking rules we just added):

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SECTION 3C: ADDITIONAL WORDPRESS SECURITY HARDENING
# Added: February 14, 2026 - Secure critical WordPress endpoints
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# Block direct access to wp-config.php from anywhere
<files wp-config.php>
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</files>

# Block access to WordPress version files (prevent version disclosure)
<FilesMatch "^(readme\.html|license\.txt|wp-config-sample\.php|liesmich\.html)$">
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</FilesMatch>

# Block access to debug.log if it exists
<Files debug.log>
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</Files>

# Limit xmlrpc.php access (blocks brute force attacks)
<Files xmlrpc.php>
    Order Deny,Allow
    Deny from all
    # If you need xmlrpc (e.g., for Jetpack), add your IP:
    # Allow from YOUR.IP.ADDRESS.HERE
</Files>

# Block access to .htaccess and .htpasswd
<FilesMatch "^\.ht">
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</FilesMatch>

# Disable directory browsing
Options -Indexes

# Block PHP execution in specific directories
<Directory "*/wp-content/uploads/">
    <FilesMatch "\.php$">
        Order Deny,Allow
        Deny from all
    </FilesMatch>
</Directory>

<Directory "*/wp-content/cache/">
    <FilesMatch "\.php$">
        Order Deny,Allow
        Deny from all
    </FilesMatch>
</Directory>

</IfModule>

# ============================================================================
# RATE LIMITING FOR ADMIN-AJAX (Prevent brute force)
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# Block suspicious admin-ajax requests (but allow legitimate ones)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/wp-admin/admin-ajax\.php [NC]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} !^https?://.*teznevisan3\.com [NC]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} (bot|spider|crawler) [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [F,L]

</IfModule>
```


## ğŸš« What NOT to Block

**NEVER block these** (will break your site):

```
âŒ /wp-admin/admin-ajax.php
âŒ /wp-json/ (REST API - needed by many plugins)
âŒ /wp-cron.php (scheduled tasks)
âŒ /wp-login.php (you need to login!)
```


## ğŸ” Better Security Options

Instead of blocking critical WordPress files, do this:

### 1. **Use WordFence to Monitor admin-ajax.php**

Already installed! Check:

- WordFence â†’ Tools â†’ Live Traffic
- Watch for suspicious admin-ajax.php patterns
- WordFence will automatically rate-limit abuse


### 2. **Disable REST API for Unauthenticated Users** (Optional)

If you don't need public REST API access, add this to your theme's `functions.php`:

```php
// Disable REST API for non-logged-in users
add_filter('rest_authentication_errors', function($result) {
    if (!empty($result)) {
        return $result;
    }
    if (!is_user_logged_in()) {
        return new WP_Error(
            'rest_not_logged_in',
            'You must be logged in to access the REST API.',
            array('status' => 401)
        );
    }
    return $result;
});
```

**âš ï¸ WARNING:** This may break some plugins! Test first.

### 3. **Hide WordPress Version**

Add to theme's `functions.php`:

```php
// Remove WordPress version from head
remove_action('wp_head', 'wp_generator');

// Remove version from RSS feeds
add_filter('the_generator', '__return_empty_string');
```


### 4. **Enable WordFence Advanced Protection**

- WordFence â†’ Firewall â†’ Enable "Extended Protection"
- Enable "Rate Limiting" for admin-ajax.php
- Set brute force protection to maximum


## ğŸ“Š Your Current Security Status

| Component | Status | Notes |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| **admin-ajax.php visible** | âœ… Normal | Required for WordPress |
| **REST API nonce visible** | âœ… Normal | Session-specific, safe |
| **wp-admin protected** | âœ… Protected | 2FA + WordFence |
| **wp-config blocked** | âœ… Blocked | In .htaccess |
| **xmlrpc blocked** | âœ… Blocked | In robots.txt |
| **Upload PHP execution** | âœ… Blocked | In .htaccess |
| **Directory browsing** | âœ… Disabled | In .htaccess |

## âœ… Recommended Actions

**DO THIS:**

1. âœ… Keep admin-ajax.php accessible (required)
2. âœ… Add Section 3C hardening rules above (optional but recommended)
3. âœ… Monitor WordFence Live Traffic for abuse
4. âœ… Enable WordFence Rate Limiting
5. âœ… Hide WordPress version (functions.php snippet above)

**DON'T DO THIS:**

1. âŒ Block admin-ajax.php (will break site)
2. âŒ Block REST API entirely (many plugins need it)
3. âŒ Block wp-cron.php (scheduled tasks won't run)

## ğŸ¯ Bottom Line

**The nonce endpoint you found is SAFE.** It's like seeing a door lock on your house - it's supposed to be visible, but it only works for the person with the right key (authentication cookies).

Your current security is **already excellent**:

- WordFence protecting admin
- 2FA enabled
- Critical files blocked
- Spam parameters blocked
- Old domains being disavowed

The additional Section 3C rules above add **extra layers** but aren't urgent. Focus on:

1. Completing the 403â†’410 fixes we discussed earlier
2. Uploading the disavow file
3. Monitoring WordFence for actual threats

You're in good shape! The visibility of admin-ajax.php is **by design**, not a vulnerability. ğŸ”’

## ğŸ› ï¸ Updated .htaccess Rules

Add these to **Section 3B** (after the rules we added earlier):

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SECTION 3D: BLOCK FAKE SHOP & PRODUCT SPAM
# Added: February 14, 2026 - Block fake e-commerce URLs
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# Block entire /shop/ directory (you don't have WooCommerce)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/shop [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block /product/edit/ spam URLs
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/product/edit/ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block language variant shop spam (en_US, fr_FR, etc.)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/[a-z]{2}_[A-Z]{2}/shop [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block /public/themes/ directory more aggressively
# This blocks HTML, MD, and other accessible files
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/public/themes/ [NC]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} \.(html|htm|md|txt|php)$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block shop query parameters (sorting/filtering spam)
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} order_by=(name|price|product_id) [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} direction=(asc|desc) [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block ?mod= parameter (appears in itm.php and shared.php spam)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)mod= [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block ?uri= parameter (contains spam like itm.php, shared.php)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)uri= [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block spam PHP files in query strings (itm.php, shared.php)
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (itm\.php|shared\.php|goods\.php|item\.php) [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

</IfModule>
```


## ğŸ“ Updated robots.txt

Add these lines to **Section 4** of your robots.txt:

```
# Block fake shop/e-commerce spam
Disallow: /shop
Disallow: /shop/
Disallow: /shop?*
Disallow: */shop
Disallow: /product/edit/
Disallow: /product/add/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /checkout/

# Block exposed theme HTML/MD files
Disallow: /public/themes/*.html
Disallow: /public/themes/*.htm
Disallow: /public/themes/*.md
Disallow: /public/themes/*.txt

# Block shop query parameters
Disallow: /*?order_by=*
Disallow: /*?mod=*
Disallow: /*?uri=*
```

## ğŸ” What This Actually Means

**"Google chose different canonical than user"** means:

- âœ… These are **likely YOUR real pages**
- âœ… Google sees them as duplicates of other pages
- âŒ Google **disagrees** with your canonical tags
- âŒ This is a **canonicalization problem**, NOT spam (mostly)

## ğŸ”§ What You Should Do Instead

### **STEP 1: Check if /shop/ is Real** (2 minutes)

Visit these URLs in your browser:

1. `https://teznevisan3.com/shop/`
2. `https://teznevisan3.com/nursing-thesis/`
3. `https://teznevisan3.com/citation/`

- â“ Do you actually HAVE a shop page?
- â“ Do you use WooCommerce or any e-commerce?
- â“ Are /nursing-thesis/ and /citation/ YOUR real service pages?


### **STEP 2: Fix Canonical Issues (The Real Problem)**

The canonical issue is likely caused by:

**A. www vs non-www confusion**

```
Problem: Google sees both as separate pages
https://teznevisan3.com/nursing-thesis/
https://www.teznevisan3.com/nursing-thesis/
```

**B. Trailing slash inconsistency**

```
Problem: Both versions exist
https://teznevisan3.com/shop
https://teznevisan3.com/shop/
```

**C. Multiple similar pages**

```
Problem: Similar content
/nursing-thesis/ and /nursing-thesis-writing/ might be too similar
```


### **STEP 3: Check Your Current Canonical Setup**

Go to one of those pages (e.g., `/nursing-thesis/`) and view source (Ctrl+U). Look for:

```html
<link rel="canonical" href="..." />
```

**Tell me:**

1. What does the canonical tag say?
2. Is it pointing to the www or non-www version?
3. Is it pointing to a different page than the current URL?

## ğŸ“Š Proper Fix Strategy

### **For Legitimate Pages:**

**1. Consolidate www vs non-www**
Add to .htaccess (if not already there):

```apache
# Force non-www (or www - pick ONE)
RewriteCond %{HTTP_HOST} ^www\.teznevisan3\.com [NC]
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://teznevisan3.com/$1 [R=301,L]
```

**2. Fix Yoast/RankMath Canonical Settings**

- WordPress Dashboard â†’ Yoast SEO (or RankMath) â†’ Settings
- Check "Canonical URLs" settings
- Make sure it's using the correct domain format

**3. Set Preferred Domain in GSC**

- This feature may have been removed in newer GSC
- But verify your sitemap only includes ONE version (www OR non-www)


### **For Actual Spam (Theme Files \& Fake Products):**

**YES, keep these blocks from earlier:**

```apache
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block fake product edit URLs

RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block spam parameters we identified

RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]
```

## ğŸ”§ Additional .htaccess Rules

Add this as **Section 3D** (after Section 3B that we prepared earlier):

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SECTION 3D: BLOCK FAKE SHOP & PRODUCT SPAM
# Added: February 14, 2026 - Block fake e-commerce URLs discovered in GSC
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# Block entire /shop/ directory and all variants (you have NO e-commerce)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/shop [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block /product/ directory (fake product pages)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/product/ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block /cart/ and /checkout/ if they appear
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/(cart|checkout) [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block language variant shop spam (en_US/shop, fr_FR/shop, etc.)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/[a-z]{2}_[A-Z]{2}/shop [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block all /public/themes/ HTML, MD, TXT files (exposed theme files)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/public/themes/ [NC]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} \.(html|htm|md|txt|php|css|js)$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block shop sorting/filtering parameters (order_by, direction)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} order_by=(name|price|product_id|date|rating) [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block ?mod= parameter (spam pattern from your GSC data)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)mod= [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block ?uri= parameter (contains spam PHP files like itm.php, shared.php)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)uri= [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block spam PHP file references in query strings
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (itm\.php|shared\.php|goods\.php|item\.php|pin\.php) [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block ?MA parameter (found in theme file spam)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)MA [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

</IfModule>
```

## ğŸ¯ About Your Removed Pages

You mentioned:
> "I had pages like /nursing-thesis/ previously and they are being removed and I am planning to create these pages again."

**For these pages, DO NOT block them!** Instead:

**1. If they're currently 404 (deleted):**

- Leave them as 404 until you recreate them
- When you recreate them, Google will re-index naturally
- The "Google chose different canonical" warning will disappear

**2. When you recreate them:**

- Make sure canonical points to itself
- Submit to GSC for re-indexing
- Ensure consistent www vs non-www usage

**3. Fix the canonical conflict:**
The issue is likely www vs non-www. Make sure your .htaccess has this (should already be there from earlier):

```apache
# Force non-www (choose ONE and stick with it)
RewriteCond %{HTTP_HOST} ^www\.teznevisan3\.com [NC]
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://teznevisan3.com/$1 [R=301,L]
```

# There is more...

For a limited time, in order to keep my website online but remove the viruses, I have designed static version of it and uploaded, links were like:
[https://www.teznevisan3.com/article-writing.html](https://www.teznevisan3.com/article-writing.html)

I want you to make all those .html pages 410 gone because they were static and are useless.

ALso, I have discovered something else:
[https://teznevisan3.com/?NA](https://teznevisan3.com/?NA)
[https://teznevisan3.com/?ND](https://teznevisan3.com/?ND)

I only saw these two links; upon click they open the home page with the same content but different URLs and it seems pages can be accessed via more than one links, I am not sure but this applies on home page it seems. Fix this issue too

Perfect detective work! These are two additional spam vectors. Let me create rules to handle both.

## ğŸ” What You Found

**1. Static HTML files** (your old emergency site):

- `*.html` pages are outdated static versions
- Need to return 410 Gone
- Should NOT redirect (just kill them)

**2. Query parameter pollution** (?NA, ?ND):

- Creates infinite duplicate URLs for same content
- Classic SEO spam technique
- Same page accessible via:
    - `https://teznevisan3.com/` (correct)
    - `https://teznevisan3.com/?NA` (duplicate)
    - `https://teznevisan3.com/?ND` (duplicate)
    - `https://teznevisan3.com/?XYZ` (probably works too!)


## ğŸ”§ Additional .htaccess Rules

Add this as **Section 3E** (after Section 3D):

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SECTION 3E: BLOCK STATIC HTML FILES & PARAMETER POLLUTION
# Added: February 14, 2026 - Remove old static site + fix query spam
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# ============================================================================
# BLOCK OLD STATIC HTML FILES (Return 410 Gone)
# ============================================================================
# Block all .html files (your old static emergency site)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} \.html$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block .htm files too (if any exist)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} \.htm$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# ============================================================================
# FIX QUERY PARAMETER POLLUTION (Strip Unknown Parameters)
# ============================================================================

# Block suspicious 2-letter uppercase query parameters (NA, ND, MA, etc.)
# These create duplicate content for homepage and other pages
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{2}$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block 3-letter uppercase parameters too (if they appear)
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{3}$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Alternative approach: Strip these parameters and redirect to clean URL
# (Use this INSTEAD of the 410 rules above if you want to preserve the page)
# RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{2,3}$ [NC]
# RewriteRule ^(.*)$ /$1? [R=301,L]

# Block any query string that's ONLY letters (no value, just ?PARAM)
# This catches ?NA, ?ND, ?ABC, etc.
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Za-z]{1,4}$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} !^(p|s|id|cat|tag)$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

</IfModule>
```


## ğŸ“ Additional robots.txt Rules

Add to **Section 4** (block spam patterns):

```
# ============================================================================
# BLOCK OLD STATIC HTML FILES
# ============================================================================
# Block all .html files (old static emergency site)
Disallow: /*.html
Disallow: /*.htm

# Block specific patterns if you remember them
Disallow: /*-writing.html
Disallow: /*-thesis.html
Disallow: /*-service.html

# ============================================================================
# BLOCK QUERY PARAMETER POLLUTION
# ============================================================================
# Block 2-3 letter uppercase parameters that create duplicates
Disallow: /*?NA
Disallow: /*?ND
Disallow: /*?MA
Disallow: /*?AB
Disallow: /*?CD
Disallow: /*?EF
Disallow: /*?GH
Disallow: /*?IJ
Disallow: /*?KL
Disallow: /*?MN
Disallow: /*?OP
Disallow: /*?QR
Disallow: /*?ST
Disallow: /*?UV
Disallow: /*?WX
Disallow: /*?YZ

# Block common single-letter spam parameters (except legitimate ones)
Disallow: /*?a=
Disallow: /*?b=
Disallow: /*?c=
Disallow: /*?d=
# Keep ?p= (WordPress post ID), ?s= (search) allowed elsewhere
```

```
â–¡ Starts with: https://teznevisan3.com/*.html

```

```
â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/article-writing.html
â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/thesis-writing.html
â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/research-writing.html
â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/proposal-writing.html
```

### **HIGH PRIORITY (Parameter pollution):**

```
â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/?ND

â–¡ https://www.teznevisan3.com/?NA

```


## ğŸ” Find All Your .html Files

To get a complete list of .html files to remove, do this:

### **Option 1: Via cPanel File Manager**

1. Login to cPanel â†’ File Manager
2. Navigate to `public_html`
3. In the search box (top right), type: `*.html`
4. List all .html files
5. Note down their names
6. Add each to GSC removals

### **Option 2: Via FTP/SSH**

If you have SSH access:

```bash
find /home/teznevi1/public_html -name "*.html" -type f
```


### **Option 3: Check Your Old Sitemap**

If you had a sitemap during the static site period, it might list all .html files.

## âš ï¸ Important Decision: 410 vs 301 Redirect

You have two options for handling query parameters like ?NA, ?ND:

### **Option A: Return 410 Gone** (Recommended)

```apache
# Kill the duplicates completely
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{2}$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]
```

âœ… **Pros:** Google removes them faster, cleaner deindexing
âŒ **Cons:** If someone bookmarked `/?NA`, they see "410 Gone"

### **Option B: Strip \& Redirect to Clean URL** (User-Friendly)

```apache
# Strip the parameter and redirect to clean URL
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{2,3}$ [NC]
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ /$1? [R=301,L]
```

âœ… **Pros:** Users still reach the page (better UX)
âœ… **Pros:** Search engines consolidate to clean URL
âŒ **Cons:** Slightly slower deindexing

**My recommendation:** Use **Option B (redirect)** for the homepage/important pages, **Option A (410)** for everything else.

## ğŸ”§ Refined .htaccess Section 3E

Here's the **BEST approach** combining both strategies:

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SECTION 3E: BLOCK STATIC HTML FILES & FIX PARAMETER POLLUTION
# Added: February 14, 2026 - Remove old static site + fix query spam
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# ============================================================================
# BLOCK OLD STATIC HTML FILES (Return 410 Gone)
# ============================================================================
# Block all .html and .htm files (old static emergency site)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} \.(html|htm)$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# ============================================================================
# FIX QUERY PARAMETER POLLUTION - SMART APPROACH
# ============================================================================

# STRATEGY 1: For homepage - Strip parameters and redirect (preserve traffic)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/index\.php$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{2,3}$ [NC]
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ /$1? [R=301,L]

# STRATEGY 2: For all other pages - Return 410 (kill duplicates)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !^/$ 
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]{2,4}$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} !^(p|s|id|cat|tag|page)$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block any single-character parameters (spam)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[A-Z]$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block numeric-only parameters (e.g., ?123, ?456)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} ^[0-9]{1,5}$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

</IfModule>
```

- âŒ /citation/ (your real page)
- âŒ /proposal-form/ (your real page)
- âŒ /research-reasoning-logic/ (your real page)

**These patterns ARE blocked:**

- âœ… /article-writing.html (old static version)
- âœ… /thesis-writing.html (old static version)
- âœ… All other .html files (temporary versions)

**Great find!** That URL shows **two issues**:

1. Complex tracking parameter chains (already mostly covered)
2. WordPress feeds that need attention

## ğŸ” Analysis of That 403 URL

```
https://teznevisan3.com/?_gl=1*1ix4f11*_gcl_au*...*_ga*...*_ga_7H42SVMQ0V*..._bdsid=...&_bd_prev_page=https://teznevisan7.com/...
```

**What's happening:**

- Multiple Google Analytics parameters chained together
- `_bd_prev_page=https://teznevisan7.com/` â†’ **Your old domain is the referrer!**
- These parameters are **already blocked** by existing .htaccess Section 8
- But the 403 â†’ 410 conversion needs one more rule


## ğŸ”§ Additional Fix Needed

Add this to **Section 3B** (after the other parameter blocks):

```apache
# Block Google Analytics 4 measurement ID parameters (pattern: _ga_XXXXXXXXX)
# Examples: _ga_7H42SVMQ0V, _ga_ABC123XYZ, etc.
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} _ga_[A-Z0-9]+ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block complex chained parameters (multiple * separators)
# Pattern: ?_gl=1*something*_gcl_au*...
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !sitemap [NC]
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} \*[a-z_]+ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]
```


## ğŸ“° WordPress Feeds - SEO Decision Guide

### **What Are These Feeds?**

| Feed URL | Purpose | SEO Value |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| `/feed/` or `/feed/rss/` | Main RSS feed (blog posts) | âœ… **KEEP** - Good for subscribers |
| `/feed/comments` | Comment RSS feed | âŒ **BLOCK** - No SEO value, creates duplicate content |
| `/feed/products` | WooCommerce product feed | âŒ **BLOCK** - You don't have WooCommerce! |

### **Why /feed/products Exists (Even Without WooCommerce)**

This is **spam or leftover code** from:

- Previous WooCommerce installation remnants
- Theme with built-in e-commerce
- Malicious code injection creating fake feeds


### **My Recommendation: Selective Blocking**

**KEEP (Good for SEO):**

- âœ… `/feed/` - Main RSS feed (if you publish blog articles)
- âœ… `/feed/rss/` - Alternative RSS format
- âœ… `/feed/atom/` - Atom feed format

**BLOCK (No SEO value / Creates spam):**

- âŒ `/feed/comments` - Comment feed (duplicate content)
- âŒ `/feed/products` - Fake product feed (you have no products!)
- âŒ `/comments/feed/` - Alternative comment feed URL
- âŒ `/*/feed/` - Individual post/page feeds (unnecessary)


## ğŸ› ï¸ Complete Feed Blocking Solution

### **Add to .htaccess Section 3F (NEW):**

```apache
# ============================================================================
# SECTION 3F: BLOCK UNNECESSARY WORDPRESS FEEDS
# Added: February 14, 2026 - Block spam/duplicate content feeds
# ============================================================================
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
RewriteEngine On

# Block /feed/products (you don't have WooCommerce - this is spam/leftover)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/feed/products/?$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block /feed/comments (no SEO value, duplicate content)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/feed/comments/?$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block /comments/feed/ (alternative comment feed URL)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/comments/feed/?$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block individual post/page comment feeds (pattern: /some-post/feed/)
# But ALLOW main /feed/ (keep for blog subscribers)
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/.+/feed/?$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !^/feed/?$ [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block feed format variations for comments
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} feed/(comments-)?rss2?/?$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} comments [NC]
RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

# Block category/tag feeds if you don't use them (optional - uncomment if needed)
# RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/category/.*/feed/?$ [NC]
# RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]
# RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/tag/.*/feed/?$ [NC]
# RewriteRule .* - [R=410,L]

</IfModule>
```


### **Add to robots.txt:**

```
# ============================================================================
# WORDPRESS FEEDS - Block unnecessary/spam feeds
# ============================================================================
# Allow main feed (good for SEO and subscribers)
Allow: /feed/
Allow: /feed/rss/
Allow: /feed/atom/

# Block spam/unnecessary feeds
Disallow: /feed/comments
Disallow: /comments/feed/
Disallow: /feed/products
Disallow: /*/feed/
Disallow: /*/comments/feed/

# Block category/tag feeds (optional - they can create duplicate content)
# Disallow: /category/*/feed/
# Disallow: /tag/*/feed/
```


### **Add to GSC Removals:**

```
CRITICAL PRIORITY:
  â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/feed/products
  â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/feed/comments
  â–¡ https://teznevisan3.com/comments/feed/
```

# I have blog posts and the feeds are redirecting to home page, especially these:

/feed/ (main RSS)
/feed/rss/
/feed/atom/

I don't know when and where I redirected the feed pages to home page because I found nothing in my rankmath.

Oh... wait... I remembered now, in the WP Code plugin, I have added 3 different sippets before so I will provide them separately; maybe they must be handled through htaccess or removed.

Code Snippets:
Clean Tracking Parameter URLs for SEO:
/**

* SEO URL Cleanup - Remove Tracking Parameters \& Fix Duplicate Content
* 
* Features:
*     - 301 redirects URLs with tracking params to clean URLs
*     - Proper canonical tags on all pages
*     - robots.txt directives to block tracking URLs
*     - Cleans internal links automatically
* 
* Plugin Name: TEZ SEO URL Cleanup
* Version: 1.0.0
*/

if (!defined('ABSPATH')) exit;

// =============================================
// CONFIGURATION - Tracking Parameters to Remove
// =============================================
function tez_get_tracking_params() {
return array(
// Google Analytics / Google Ads
'_gl',
'_ga',
'_gac',
'_gcl_au',
'_gcl_aw',
'_gcl_dc',
'_gclid',
'gclid',
'gclsrc',
'_gid',
'dclid',
'wbraid',
'gbraid',

        // Facebook / Meta
        'fbclid',
        'fb_action_ids',
        'fb_action_types',
        'fb_source',
        'fb_ref',
        
        // Microsoft / Bing
        'msclkid',
        
        // Custom / Third-party tracking (from your example)
        '_bdsid',
        '_bd_prev_page',
        
        // Email Marketing
        'mc_cid',
        'mc_eid',
        
        // HubSpot
        '_hsenc',
        '_hsmi',
        '__hstc',
        '__hsfp',
        'hsCtaTracking',
        
        // Marketo
        'mkt_tok',
        
        // Affiliate / Other
        'zanpid',
        'irclickid',
        'clickid',
        '_ke',
        'trk_contact',
        'trk_msg',
        'trk_module',
        'trk_sid',
        
        // Session tracking
        'sessionid',
        'phpsessid',
        
        // Misc tracking
        'ref',
        'ref_',
        'affiliate_id',
        'partner_id',
        
        // Uncomment below to also remove UTM params
        // 'utm_source',
        // 'utm_medium',
        // 'utm_campaign',
        // 'utm_term',
        // 'utm_content',
        // 'utm_id',
    );
    }

// =============================================
// 301 REDIRECT: Clean Tracking Parameters
// =============================================
function tez_clean_tracking_redirect() {
// Skip in admin, AJAX, cron, CLI, REST API, XML-RPC
if (
is_admin() ||
wp_doing_ajax() ||
defined('DOING_CRON') ||
defined('WP_CLI') ||
defined('REST_REQUEST') ||
(defined('XMLRPC_REQUEST') \&\& XMLRPC_REQUEST) ||
(defined('DOING_AUTOSAVE') \&\& DOING_AUTOSAVE)
) {
return;
}

    // Get request URI
    $request_uri = isset($_SERVER['REQUEST_URI']) ? $_SERVER['REQUEST_URI'] : '';
    
    // No query string = nothing to clean
    if (strpos($request_uri, '?') === false) {
        return;
    }
    
    // Parse URL
    $parsed_url = parse_url($request_uri);
    
    if (empty($parsed_url['query'])) {
        return;
    }
    
    // Parse query parameters
    parse_str($parsed_url['query'], $query_params);
    
    if (empty($query_params) || !is_array($query_params)) {
        return;
    }
    
    // Get tracking params list
    $tracking_params = tez_get_tracking_params();
    
    // Filter out tracking parameters
    $found_tracking = false;
    $clean_params = array();
    
    foreach ($query_params as $key => $value) {
        $is_tracking = false;
        $key_lower = strtolower($key);
        
        // Check each tracking parameter
        foreach ($tracking_params as $tracking_param) {
            $param_lower = strtolower($tracking_param);
            
            // Exact match
            if ($key_lower === $param_lower) {
                $is_tracking = true;
                break;
            }
            
            // Prefix match for params like _ga_XXXXX, _gcl_XX
            if (strpos($key_lower, $param_lower . '_') === 0 || strpos($key_lower, $param_lower) === 0) {
                // Check if it's actually a prefix (not just coincidence)
                if (strlen($key_lower) > strlen($param_lower)) {
                    $next_char = substr($key_lower, strlen($param_lower), 1);
                    if ($next_char === '_' || $next_char === '' || ctype_alnum($next_char)) {
                        $is_tracking = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        if ($is_tracking) {
            $found_tracking = true;
        } else {
            $clean_params[$key] = $value;
        }
    }
    
    // If tracking params found, redirect to clean URL
    if ($found_tracking) {
        // Build clean path
        $path = isset($parsed_url['path']) ? $parsed_url['path'] : '/';
        
        // Ensure path is not empty
        if (empty($path)) {
            $path = '/';
        }
        
        // Build clean URL
        $clean_url = $path;
        
        // Add remaining params if any
        if (!empty($clean_params)) {
            $clean_url .= '?' . http_build_query($clean_params, '', '&', PHP_QUERY_RFC3986);
        }
        
        // Build full URL
        $scheme = is_ssl() ? 'https' : 'http';
        $host = isset($_SERVER['HTTP_HOST']) ? sanitize_text_field($_SERVER['HTTP_HOST']) : parse_url(home_url(), PHP_URL_HOST);
        
        $full_clean_url = $scheme . '://' . $host . $clean_url;
        
        // Prevent redirect loops - compare normalized URLs
        $current_url = $scheme . '://' . $host . $request_uri;
        
        if (strtolower($full_clean_url) === strtolower($current_url)) {
            return;
        }
        
        // Safety check - don't redirect if URL looks malformed
        if (empty($host) || strlen($full_clean_url) > 2000) {
            return;
        }
        
        // Perform 301 permanent redirect
        if (!headers_sent()) {
            // Remove any existing headers that might interfere
            header_remove('Location');
            
            // Set cache headers for this redirect
            header('Cache-Control: max-age=31536000'); // 1 year
            header('X-Redirect-Reason: Tracking parameters removed for SEO');
            
            // Perform redirect
            wp_redirect($full_clean_url, 301);
            exit;
        }
    }
    }
add_action('template_redirect', 'tez_clean_tracking_redirect', 1);

// Also run earlier to catch more cases
add_action('init', function() {
if (!is_admin()) {
tez_clean_tracking_redirect();
}
}, 1);

// =============================================
// CANONICAL TAG - Clean \& Proper
// =============================================
function tez_setup_clean_canonical() {
if (is_admin()) {
return;
}

    // Remove WordPress default canonical
    remove_action('wp_head', 'rel_canonical');
    
    // Remove Yoast canonical if exists (we'll handle it)
    add_filter('wpseo_canonical', 'tez_filter_canonical_url', 999);
    
    // Remove RankMath canonical if exists
    add_filter('rank_math/frontend/canonical', 'tez_filter_canonical_url', 999);
    
    // Add our clean canonical
    add_action('wp_head', 'tez_output_clean_canonical', 1);
    }
add_action('wp', 'tez_setup_clean_canonical');

function tez_filter_canonical_url($url) {
    if (empty($url)) {
return \$url;
}
return remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), \$url);
}

function tez_output_clean_canonical() {
\$canonical = tez_get_current_canonical();

    if ($canonical && !is_wp_error($canonical)) {
        // Remove any tracking params from canonical
        $canonical = remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), $canonical);
        
        // Ensure proper URL format
        $canonical = esc_url($canonical);
        
        if (!empty($canonical)) {
            echo '<link rel="canonical" href="' . $canonical . '" />' . "\\n";
        }
    }
    }

function tez_get_current_canonical() {
\$canonical = '';

    if (is_singular()) {
        $canonical = wp_get_canonical_url();
        if (!$canonical) {
            $canonical = get_permalink();
        }
    } elseif (is_home() && !is_front_page()) {
        $canonical = get_permalink(get_option('page_for_posts'));
    } elseif (is_front_page()) {
        $canonical = home_url('/');
    } elseif (is_category()) {
        $canonical = get_category_link(get_queried_object_id());
    } elseif (is_tag()) {
        $canonical = get_tag_link(get_queried_object_id());
    } elseif (is_tax()) {
        $term = get_queried_object();
        if ($term) {
            $canonical = get_term_link($term);
        }
    } elseif (is_post_type_archive()) {
        $canonical = get_post_type_archive_link(get_post_type());
    } elseif (is_author()) {
        $canonical = get_author_posts_url(get_queried_object_id());
    } elseif (is_date()) {
        if (is_day()) {
            $canonical = get_day_link(get_the_date('Y'), get_the_date('m'), get_the_date('d'));
        } elseif (is_month()) {
            $canonical = get_month_link(get_the_date('Y'), get_the_date('m'));
        } elseif (is_year()) {
            $canonical = get_year_link(get_the_date('Y'));
        }
    } elseif (is_search()) {
        $canonical = get_search_link(get_search_query());
    }
    
    // Handle pagination
    $paged = get_query_var('paged');
    if ($paged > 1 && $canonical) {
        if (strpos($canonical, '?') !== false) {
            $canonical = add_query_arg('paged', $paged, $canonical);
        } else {
            $canonical = trailingslashit($canonical) . 'page/' . $paged . '/';
        }
    }
    
    return $canonical;
    }

// =============================================
// ROBOTS.TXT - Block Tracking URLs
// =============================================
function tez_robots_txt_additions(\$output, $public) {
    if (!$public) {
return \$output;
}

    $additions = "\\n";
    $additions .= "# =============================================\\n";
    $additions .= "# Block crawling of URLs with tracking parameters\\n";
    $additions .= "# Added by TEZ SEO URL Cleanup\\n";
    $additions .= "# =============================================\\n\\n";
    
    // Disallow tracking parameter URLs
    $additions .= "# Google Analytics / Ads tracking\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_gl=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_ga=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_gac=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_gcl*=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*gclid=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*gclsrc=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*dclid=*\\n";
    
    $additions .= "\\n# Facebook tracking\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*fbclid=*\\n";
    
    $additions .= "\\n# Microsoft / Bing tracking\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*msclkid=*\\n";
    
    $additions .= "\\n# Custom tracking parameters\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_bdsid=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_bd_prev_page=*\\n";
    
    $additions .= "\\n# HubSpot tracking\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_hsenc=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*_hsmi=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*__hstc=*\\n";
    
    $additions .= "\\n# Email marketing tracking\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*mc_cid=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*mc_eid=*\\n";
    $additions .= "Disallow: /*?*mkt_tok=*\\n";
    
    // Clean-param directive (for Yandex and some other bots)
    $additions .= "\\n# Clean-param directive for Yandex\\n";
    $additions .= "Clean-param: _gl&_ga&_gac&_gcl_au&_gcl_aw&gclid&fbclid&_bdsid&_bd_prev_page&msclkid&_hsenc&_hsmi&__hstc&mc_cid&mc_eid\\n";
    
    return $output . $additions;
    }
add_filter('robots_txt', 'tez_robots_txt_additions', 999, 2);

// =============================================
// CLEAN INTERNAL LINKS AUTOMATICALLY
// =============================================
function tez_clean_internal_links($url) {
    // Only process internal links
    if (empty($url)) {
return \$url;
}

    $site_host = parse_url(home_url(), PHP_URL_HOST);
    $url_host = parse_url($url, PHP_URL_HOST);
    
    // Skip external URLs
    if ($url_host && $url_host !== $site_host) {
        return $url;
    }
    
    // Remove tracking params
    return remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), $url);
    }

// Apply to various link filters
add_filter('the_permalink', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('post_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('page_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('term_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('post_type_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('attachment_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('year_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('month_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('day_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('category_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('tag_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);
add_filter('author_link', 'tez_clean_internal_links', 999);

// =============================================
// HTTP LINK HEADER FOR CANONICAL
// =============================================
function tez_add_canonical_http_header() {
if (is_admin() || headers_sent() || wp_doing_ajax()) {
return;
}

    $canonical = tez_get_current_canonical();
    
    if ($canonical && !is_wp_error($canonical)) {
        $canonical = remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), $canonical);
        header('Link: <' . esc_url($canonical) . '>; rel="canonical"', false);
    }
    }
add_action('send_headers', 'tez_add_canonical_http_header', 999);

// =============================================
// CLEAN REDIRECT URLs
// =============================================
function tez_clean_redirect_url(\$location) {
// Only clean internal redirects
\$site_host = parse_url(home_url(), PHP_URL_HOST);
$redirect_host = parse_url($location, PHP_URL_HOST);

    if (!$redirect_host || $redirect_host === $site_host) {
        return remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), $location);
    }
    
    return $location;
    }
add_filter('wp_redirect', 'tez_clean_redirect_url', 999);

// =============================================
// CLEAN REST API LINKS
// =============================================
function tez_clean_rest_url(\$url) {
return remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), \$url);
}
add_filter('rest_url', 'tez_clean_rest_url', 999);

// =============================================
// CLEAN SITEMAPS (if using WordPress core sitemap)
// =============================================
function tez_clean_sitemap_url(\$url) {
return remove_query_arg(tez_get_tracking_params(), $url);
}
add_filter('wp_sitemaps_posts_entry', function($entry) {
if (isset(\$entry['loc'])) {
$entry['loc'] = tez_clean_sitemap_url($entry['loc']);
}
return \$entry;
}, 999);

add_filter('wp_sitemaps_taxonomies_entry', function($entry) {
    if (isset($entry['loc'])) {
$entry['loc'] = tez_clean_sitemap_url($entry['loc']);
}
return \$entry;
}, 999);

// =============================================
// ADMIN NOTICE - Confirmation
// =============================================
function tez_seo_cleanup_admin_notice() {
if (!current_user_can('manage_options')) {
return;
}

    // Only show on dashboard and SEO-related pages
    $screen = get_current_screen();
    if (!$screen || !in_array($screen->id, array('dashboard', 'options-general', 'options-reading'))) {
        return;
    }
    
    // Check if this is the first time showing
    $dismissed = get_option('tez_seo_cleanup_notice_dismissed', false);
    if ($dismissed) {
        return;
    }
    
    ?>
    <div class="notice notice-success is-dismissible" id="tez-seo-cleanup-notice">
        <p>
            ```
            <strong>âœ… TEZ SEO URL Cleanup Active</strong> - 
            ```
            ```
            URLs with tracking parameters (<code>_gl</code>, <code>_ga</code>, <code>_bdsid</code>, <code>fbclid</code>, etc.) 
            ```
            are now being 301 redirected to clean canonical URLs.
        </p>
    </div>
    <script>
    jQuery(document).on('click', '#tez-seo-cleanup-notice .notice-dismiss', function() {
        jQuery.post(ajaxurl, {
            action: 'tez_dismiss_seo_cleanup_notice',
            nonce: '<?php echo wp_create_nonce('tez_dismiss_notice'); ?>'
        });
    });
    </script>
    <?php
    }
add_action('admin_notices', 'tez_seo_cleanup_admin_notice');

function tez_dismiss_seo_cleanup_notice() {
if (!wp_verify_nonce(\$_POST['nonce'], 'tez_dismiss_notice')) {
wp_die();
}
update_option('tez_seo_cleanup_notice_dismissed', true);
wp_die();
}
add_action('wp_ajax_tez_dismiss_seo_cleanup_notice', 'tez_dismiss_seo_cleanup_notice');

* Return 404 for author archive pages
* This completely removes author archives from your site [[9]]

function tez_disable_author_archives() {
if (is_author()) {
global \$wp_query;
\$wp_query->set_404();
status_header(404);
nocache_headers();

     // Load 404 template if exists
     $template = get_404_template();
     if ($template) {
         include($template);
         exit;
     }
    }
}

/**

function tez_jannah_filter_post_meta($meta) {

// Keep author but ensure no link
\$meta['author_link'] = false;
}
return \$meta;

// =============================================
// 4. REMOVE AUTHOR LINKS VIA OUTPUT BUFFER
// =============================================

/**

* Fallback: Remove author links from rendered HTML
* This catches any author links that slip through filters
*/
add_action('wp_loaded', 'tez_start_author_link_buffer');
function tez_start_author_link_buffer() {
if (!is_admin()) {
ob_start('tez_remove_author_links_from_html');
}
}

function tez_remove_author_links_from_html(\$html) {
// Pattern to match author archive links
\$patterns = array(
// Match links to /author/username/
'/<a\\s+[^>]*href=["\\'][^"\\']*\\/author\\/[^"\\']*["\\'][^>]*>(.*?)<\\/a>/is',
// Match links with rel="author"
'/<a\\s+[^>]*rel=["\\']author["\\'][^>]*>(.*?)<\\/a>/is',
);

    foreach ($patterns as $pattern) {
        $html = preg_replace_callback($pattern, function($matches) {
            // Return just the text content wrapped in a span
            ```
            return '<span class="author-name">' . strip_tags($matches[1]) . '</span>';
            ```
        }, $html);
    }
    
    return $html;
    }

// =============================================
// 5. REMOVE AUTHOR FROM REST API \& FEEDS
// =============================================

/**

* Remove author information from REST API responses
*/
add_filter('rest_prepare_post', 'tez_remove_author_from_rest', 10, 3);
function tez_remove_author_from_rest(\$response, \$post, $request) {
 // Remove author link from REST API
 if (isset($response->data['_links']['author'])) {
unset(\$response->data['_links']['author']);
}
return \$response;
}

* Remove author archives from XML sitemap

 if ($name === 'users') {
return false;
}
return \$provider;
}

}
return \$author;
}

// =============================================
// 6. REMOVE AUTHOR LINK FROM HEAD
// =============================================

* Remove author link from document head

/**

* Remove author meta tags
*/
add_action('wp_head', 'tez_remove_author_meta', 1);
function tez_remove_author_meta() {
// Remove via output buffer for head section
ob_start(function(\$output) {
// Remove author meta tags
\$output = preg_replace('/<link[^>]*rel=["\\']author["\\'][^>]*>/i', '', \$output);
\$output = preg_replace('/<meta[^>]*name=["\\']author["\\'][^>]*>/i', '', \$output);
return \$output;
});
}

ob_end_flush();
}, 999);

function tez_author_link_css() {
?>
<style id="tez-disable-author-links">
/* Make any remaining author links non-clickable */
a[href*="/author/"],
a[rel="author"],
.post-meta a[href*="/author/"],
.entry-meta a[href*="/author/"],
.tie-post-meta a[href*="/author/"],
.author-box a[href*="/author/"],
.meta-info a[href*="/author/"] {
pointer-events: none !important;
cursor: default !important;
color: inherit !important;
text-decoration: none !important;
}

    /* Style the author name span */
    .author-name {
        font-weight: inherit;
        color: inherit;
    }
    
    /* Keep author box visible but remove link styling */
    .author-box,
    .tie-author-box,
    .single-post-meta .author,
    .post-author {
        display: block;
    }
    
    .author-box a[href*="/author/"],
    .tie-author-box a[href*="/author/"] {
        pointer-events: none !important;
        text-decoration: none !important;
    }
    </style>
    <?php
    }

// =============================================
// 8. BLOCK AUTHOR ENUMERATION (SECURITY)
// =============================================

/**

* Prevent author enumeration via ?author=1 queries
* Security measure to prevent user discovery
*/
add_action('template_redirect', 'tez_block_author_enumeration');
function tez_block_author_enumeration() {
if (isset(\$_GET['author']) \&\& !is_admin()) {
wp_safe_redirect(home_url('/'), 301);
exit;
}
}

/**

* Remove author query var
*/
add_filter('query_vars', 'tez_remove_author_query_var');
function tez_remove_author_query_var(\$vars) {
if (!is_admin()) {
\$key = array_search('author', $vars);
     if ($key !== false) {
unset($vars[$key]);
}
\$key = array_search('author_name', $vars);
     if ($key !== false) {
unset($vars[$key]);
}
}
return \$vars;
}

* Disable author archives in Yoast SEO
*/
add_filter('wpseo_author_archive', '__return_false');

/**

* Disable author archives in Rank Math
*/
add_filter('rank_math/sitemap/exclude_author', '__return_true');

/**

* Remove author from Yoast schema
*/
add_filter('wpseo_schema_graph_pieces', 'tez_remove_author_schema', 10, 2);
function tez_remove_author_schema(\$pieces, $context) {
 return array_filter($pieces, function($piece) {
     return !($piece instanceof \\Yoast\\WP\\SEO\\Generators\\Schema\\Author);
});
}

Disable Feed:
// Redirect all feed requests to the original post URL (without feed)
function disable_and_redirect_feeds() {
if (is_feed()) {
wp_redirect(home_url( add_query_arg( array(),\$wp->request ) ), 301);
exit();
}
}
add_action('template_redirect', 'disable_and_redirect_feeds');

add_filter('feed_links_show_posts_feed', '__return_false');
add_filter('feed_links_show_comments_feed', '__return_false');

// Disable the RSS feeds entirely by killing feed requests
function disable_rss_feed_access() {
if (is_feed()) {
wp_die(__('No feed available', 'textdomain'), '', array('response' => 404));
}
}
add_action('template_redirect', 'disable_rss_feed_access');

**Critical Issues Found!** Your robots.txt has **invalid syntax** that's breaking GSC validation. Let me fix everything:

## ğŸ” Problems Identified

1. **Invalid Directive (Line 29):** `Content-Signal: search=yes,ai-train=no` - This is NOT valid robots.txt syntax!
2. **Regex Not Supported:** `/*.html$`, `/*.php$`, `/*?[A-Z]` - The `$` and `[A-Z]` are regex, not robots.txt
3. **Conflicting Rules:** `Disallow: /feed/` then `Allow: /feed/` - Creates conflict
4. **Different Files:** HTTP vs HTTPS versions have different content (bad!)
5. **22 GSC Errors:** Multiple syntax violations

## ğŸ¤– AI Crawler Strategy

Since you want **AI visibility** for AEO/AIO/GEO, I'll:

- âœ… **ALLOW** all major AI crawlers (GPTBot, Google-Extended, ClaudeBot, etc.)
- âœ… Keep content accessible for AI training
- âœ… Only block spam/security threats
- âœ… Optimize for both SEO and AI discovery

## ğŸ“‹ **How to Set Up in cPanel:**

### **Step 1: Access Auto-Responders**

1. Log in to cPanel
2. Find **"Email"** section
3. Click **"Autoresponders"**

### **Step 2: Create New Auto-Responder**

1. Click **"Add Autoresponder"**
2. **Character Set:** UTF-8 (for Persian support)
3. **Interval:** 4 hours (prevents spam if someone emails multiple times)
4. **Email:** Select your email (inquiry@teznevisan3.com or whatever receives messages)
5. **From:** Teznevisan Institute
6. **Subject (English):** Your Message Has Been Received - Teznevisan Institute âœ“
7. **Subject (Persian):** Ù¾ÛŒØ§Ù… Ø´Ù…Ø§ Ø¯Ø±ÛŒØ§ÙØª Ø´Ø¯ - Ù…ÙˆØ³Ø³Ù‡ ØªØ²Ù†ÙˆÛŒØ³Ø§Ù† âœ“
8. **Body:**
    - Switch to **HTML mode** (if available)
    - Paste the entire HTML code above
9. **Start/Stop:** Set appropriate dates (or leave for continuous)
10. Click **"Create"**

### **Step 3: Test**

- Send a test email to your address
- Check if auto-reply arrives
- Verify Persian/English display correctly
- Check all links work

## ğŸš€ **Why This Will Work:**

Most markdown parsers require a **blank line** between headers and lists. Without it, they interpret the bullets as part of the header, not as a separate list!

**This is standard markdown formatting** - the validator follows strict markdown rules!

## ğŸ¯ **FOUND THE REAL PROBLEM!**

The validator was looking for **MARKDOWN HYPERLINKS** in format `[Text](URL)`, not bare URLs!

***

## ğŸ“¦ **Download: [llms.txt](code_file:62) - CORRECT FORMAT**


***

## âŒ **What Was Wrong:**

Your file had URLs like this:

```markdown
- **Master Thesis:** Complete service - https://teznevisan3.com/service/
```

**The validator couldn't recognize these as "markdown hyperlinks"!**

***

## âœ… **What's Fixed:**

Now using proper markdown link format:

```markdown
- [Master Thesis Writing](https://teznevisan3.com/service/) - Complete service
```


***

## ğŸ”§ **Key Changes:**

| Before (Wrong) | After (Correct) |
| :-- | :-- |
| `Text - https://url` | `[Text](https://url) - Description` |
| `Email: address` | `[Email](mailto:address)` |
| `Phone: number` | `[Phone](tel:number)` |
| Bare URLs | Markdown hyperlinks |


***

## âœ… **Validator Requirements Met:**

1. âœ… **H1 title** with project name
2. âœ… **Blockquote summary**
3. âœ… **H2 sections** with list items
4. âœ… **MARKDOWN HYPERLINKS** `[Text](URL)` â† **This was missing!**
5. âœ… **Email links** `[email](mailto:email)`
6. âœ… **Phone links** `[tel](tel:number)`
7. âœ… Blank lines after H2
8. âœ… No H3 subsections

***

## ğŸ“¦ **Download: [llms.txt](code_file:62) - LLMSTXT.ORG COMPLIANT**


***

## ğŸ”‘ **The Critical Requirement I Found:**

According to [llmstxt.org specification](https://www.answer.ai/posts/2024-09-03-llmstxt.html):

> **"Each 'file list' is a markdown list, containing a required markdown hyperlink `[name](url)`, then optionally a `:` and notes about the file."**

### **EVERY list item MUST follow this EXACT format:**

```markdown
- [name](url): optional description
```


***

## âŒ **What You CANNOT Have:**

```markdown
- **Bold text:** description (NO URL = ERROR!)
- Plain text without link (ERROR!)
- Text - https://url.com (Wrong format!)
```


## âœ… **What You MUST Have:**

```markdown
- [Link Text](https://url.com): Description here
- [Another Link](https://url.com): More description
- [Email](mailto:email@site.com): Contact information
```


***

## ğŸ“Š **File Structure (Compliant):**

```markdown
# Teznevisan Institute

> Iran's #1 Assignment Help & Academic Research Institute Since 2013...

## About

- [About Teznevisan Institute](https://teznevisan3.com/about/): Founded 2013, oldest specialized thesis consulting firm
- [Career Opportunities](https://teznevisan3.com/hiring/): Join our team of 40+ PhD researchers
- [Customer Feedback](https://teznevisan3.com/complaint/): Submit feedback and testimonials

## Contact

- [Contact Us Page](https://teznevisan3.com/contact-us/): Main contact page with office address
- [Online Inquiry Form](https://teznevisan3.com/inquiry/): Submit your project inquiry online 24/7
- [WhatsApp Persian Speakers](https://wa.me/09331663849): Primary contact for Iranian students
- [Telegram Persian Speakers](https://t.me/Thesissupport): Direct support channel
- [English Coordinator Email](mailto:maziyarid@gmail.com): Maziyar Moradi connects English speakers with field experts
- [General Email](mailto:inquiry@teznevisan3.com): General inquiries in any language

## Services

- [Master Thesis Writing](https://teznevisan3.com/writing-thesis/master/): Complete thesis with 97% approval rate
- [PhD Dissertation Writing](https://teznevisan3.com/writing-thesis/phd/): Original research with advanced analysis
- [ISI Papers](https://teznevisan3.com/writing-paper/isi/): Web of Science Q1/Q2 journal targeting
... (21 service links total)

## Software and Tools

- [SPSS Analysis](https://teznevisan3.com/statistical-analysis/spss/): Descriptive statistics, ANOVA, regression
- [Stata Analysis](https://teznevisan3.com/stata/): Econometrics, panel data, time series
... (18 software links total)

## Research Methodologies

- [Complete Research Methodology Guide](https://teznevisan3.com/research-methodology/): Comprehensive guide
- [Qualitative Research Methods](https://teznevisan3.com/qualitative-method/): Phenomenology, grounded theory
... (8 methodology links total)

## Educational Resources

- [How to Write a Thesis](https://teznevisan3.com/how-to-write-thesis/): Complete step-by-step guide
- [How to Write Review Papers](https://teznevisan3.com/how-to-write-review-paper/): Systematic review guide
... (16 resource links total)

## Website Structure

- [Homepage](https://teznevisan3.com): Main website with service overview
- [Complete Sitemap](https://teznevisan3.com/sitemap_index.xml): XML sitemap index
- [Privacy Policy](https://teznevisan3.com/privacy-policy-2/): Data protection information
```

## âœ… **What This File Has:**

| Requirement | Status |
| :-- | :-- |
| H1 title | âœ… `# Teznevisan Institute` |
| Blockquote summary | âœ… 2 sentences about institute |
| H2 sections | âœ… 7 sections |
| List items with links | âœ… 77 items, ALL with `[name](url): description` |
| No plain text bullets | âœ… Every bullet has a URL |
| No bullets without links | âœ… All links properly formatted |
| Blank lines after H2 | âœ… Proper spacing |
| UTF-8 encoding | âœ… For international content |


***

## ğŸ¯ **Why This Will Pass:**

1. **Every single list item** has a markdown link `[text](url)`
2. **No plain text** bullets without URLs
3. **Proper format:** `- [name](url): description`
4. **Follows spec exactly** from llmstxt.org

# Validated. Now should we add it to robots.txt? I fetched it on SC but how about others?

Excellent! **Validation passed!** ğŸ‰ Now let's get it discovered by all AI systems.

## ğŸ¤– **robots.txt - YES, Add a Sitemap Entry**

Add this line to your **robots.txt**:

```
Sitemap: https://teznevisan3.com/sitemap_index.xml
```

**Why?** Even though you already have sitemaps, explicitly declaring it in robots.txt helps AI crawlers (GPTBot, ClaudeBot, etc.) discover your llms.txt faster through the sitemap.

### **Your Complete robots.txt Should Include:**

```
User-agent: *
Disallow: /wp-admin/
Allow: /wp-admin/admin-ajax.php
Disallow: /wp-includes/
Disallow: /wp-content/plugins/
Disallow: /wp-content/cache/
Disallow: /?s=
Disallow: /search/

# AI Crawlers - Allow All
User-agent: GPTBot
Allow: /

User-agent: ChatGPT-User
Allow: /

User-agent: ClaudeBot
Allow: /

User-agent: Claude-Web
Allow: /

User-agent: PerplexityBot
Allow: /

User-agent: Google-Extended
Allow: /

User-agent: CCBot
Allow: /

User-agent: anthropic-ai
Allow: /

User-agent: Bytespider
Allow: /

# Sitemaps
Sitemap: https://teznevisan3.com/sitemap_index.xml
Sitemap: https://teznevisan3.com/llms.txt

# Optional but helpful
User-agent: *
Allow: /llms.txt
```

**Note:** You can actually list `llms.txt` as a "sitemap" since it's a discovery file!

## **Step 1: Report to Google Via Product Policy Violations** âš ï¸

Google said: *"If you believe the content in question may violate our product policies"* - **This is your path!**

### **A. Report Copyright/Trademark Violation (Public Form)**

**Go to:** https://support.google.com/legal/troubleshooter/1114905

**Select:**

1. âœ… "Trademark"
2. âœ… "Google Search"
3. Fill out the form with:
```
Trademark: Teznevisan / Ù…ÙˆØ³Ø³Ù‡ ØªØ²Ù†ÙˆÛŒØ³Ø§Ù†
Your Website: https://teznevisan3.com
Established: 2013
Registration: [If you have Iranian trademark registration number, include it]

Infringing Website: https://teznevisan.ir
```

## **Step 2: Iranian Domain Dispute Resolution** ğŸ‡®ğŸ‡·

```
- Name: Teznevisan Institute (Ù…ÙˆØ³Ø³Ù‡ ØªØ²Ù†ÙˆÛŒØ³Ø§Ù†)

Registrant: [Check Whois]

Grounds for Dispute:
1. Trademark Infringement: "Teznevisan" is our established brand since 2013
2. Bad Faith Registration: Registered to profit from our brand recognition
3. Confusing Similarity: Exact match to our trademark
4. Customer Confusion: Our clients are being misled to their website

Evidence:
- Our business operating since 2013 (13 years)
- Their domain registered recently (after our brand established)
- SEO targeting our brand keywords
- Customer confusion reports

Relief Requested:
- Transfer of teznevisan.ir domain to rightful owner (us)
- OR suspension of teznevisan.ir domain

Iranian Law References:
- Law on Registration of Trademarks and Inventions
- Electronic Commerce Law Article [relevant article]
- Unfair Competition provisions

Attached Documents:
1. Business registration certificate
2. Domain registration proof (teznevisan3.com since 2013)

[Your phone]
```

# One question, if I create an English version of my website and create some pages which will be multilingual, but not only for SEO purposes, but for attracting those who search in English and seeking an institute in Iran, as well as AI recognition, does it hurt my Persian SEO if I do so? Or should I create a subdomain for this purpose?

**Excellent question!** Adding English content will **NOT hurt your Persian SEO** if done correctly. In fact, it will **HELP** your overall authority and AI recognition. Let me break this down:

***

## ğŸ¯ **Direct Answer: Same Domain vs Subdomain**

### **âœ… RECOMMENDED: Same Domain with Language Folders**

**Structure:**

```
teznevisan3.com/         â†’ Persian (default)
teznevisan3.com/en/      â†’ English version
teznevisan3.com/ar/      â†’ Arabic (future)
```

**Why This is BEST:**

âœ… **Doesn't hurt Persian SEO** - Google/AI treats as separate language versions
âœ… **Consolidates domain authority** - All backlinks benefit main domain
âœ… **Better for AI systems** - Single domain = stronger entity recognition
âœ… **Easier maintenance** - One WordPress installation
âœ… **Better user experience** - Easy language switching
âœ… **Stronger brand** - teznevisan3.com becomes multilingual powerhouse

***

### **âŒ NOT RECOMMENDED: Subdomain**

**Structure:**

```
teznevisan3.com    â†’ Persian
en.teznevisan3.com â†’ English
```

**Why Avoid:**

âŒ **Splits authority** - Google treats as separate sites
âŒ **Divides SEO value** - Backlinks don't fully transfer
âŒ **Confuses AI** - Two separate entities instead of one
âŒ **More technical work** - Separate SSL, separate setup
âŒ **Weaker brand** - Less cohesive

**Only use subdomain if:** You're creating a completely different business/brand

***

## ğŸ“Š **Impact on Persian SEO: Will It Hurt?**

### **Short Answer: NO! Here's why:**

**1. Google Understands Language Separation**

- Persian content ranks for Persian queries
- English content ranks for English queries
- They don't compete with each other
- Using `hreflang` tags tells Google which is which

**2. Actually HELPS Your Persian SEO**

- More content = more authority
- English backlinks boost domain authority
- Domain authority helps ALL languages
- More pages = more internal linking opportunities

**3. AI Systems LOVE Multilingual Content**

- Shows broader reach and authority
- AI can recommend you to English speakers AND Persian speakers
- Demonstrates international capability
- Better entity understanding

***

## ğŸ”§ **How to Implement Without Hurting Persian SEO**

### **Step 1: Choose URL Structure**

**Option A: Subfolder (RECOMMENDED)** â­

```
teznevisan3.com/           â†’ Persian homepage
teznevisan3.com/about/     â†’ Persian about
teznevisan3.com/services/  â†’ Persian services

teznevisan3.com/en/        â†’ English homepage
teznevisan3.com/en/about/  â†’ English about
teznevisan3.com/en/services/ â†’ English services
```

**Pros:**

- âœ… Simple to implement
- âœ… Single domain authority
- âœ… Easy language switcher
- âœ… Best for AI recognition
- âœ… Standard practice globally

**Option B: Language Parameter (Alternative)**

```
teznevisan3.com/?lang=fa   â†’ Persian
teznevisan3.com/?lang=en   â†’ English
```

**Pros:**

- âœ… Very simple
- âœ… Same domain

**Cons:**

- âŒ Less clean URLs
- âŒ Not as SEO-friendly

**Verdict: Use Option A (Subfolder)**

***

### **Step 2: Implement hreflang Tags** (CRITICAL!)

This tells Google/Bing which language version is which.

**On Persian pages, add:**

```html
<link rel="alternate" hreflang="fa" href="https://teznevisan3.com/" />
<link rel="alternate" hreflang="en" href="https://teznevisan3.com/en/" />
<link rel="alternate" hreflang="x-default" href="https://teznevisan3.com/" />
```

**On English pages, add:**

```html
<link rel="alternate" hreflang="fa" href="https://teznevisan3.com/" />
<link rel="alternate" hreflang="en" href="https://teznevisan3.com/en/" />
<link rel="alternate" hreflang="x-default" href="https://teznevisan3.com/" />
```

**`x-default`** = Default for users who don't match other languages (use Persian as default)

***

### **Step 3: Use WordPress Multilingual Plugins**

**Best Options:**

**1. WPML (Recommended)** - \$39/year

- Professional multilingual solution
- Automatic hreflang tags
- Easy translation management
- SEO-optimized
- Used by major sites

**2. Polylang (Free)**

- Good free alternative
- Manual translations
- Works well with most themes
- Need Polylang Pro for automatic hreflang

**3. TranslatePress (Free/Pro)**

- Visual translation editor
- User-friendly
- Good for beginners

**Installation Steps with WPML:**

1. Install WPML plugin
2. Set Persian as default language
3. Add English as secondary language
4. Choose subfolder structure (/en/)
5. Translate pages/posts
6. WPML handles hreflang automatically

***

### **Step 4: Proper Language Targeting**

**Set language in HTML tag:**

**Persian pages:**

```html
<html lang="fa" dir="rtl">
```

**English pages:**

```html
<html lang="en" dir="ltr">
```

This helps Google AND screen readers.

***

### **Step 5: Internal Linking Strategy**

**Link between language versions:**

- Add language switcher in header/footer
- Shows flags or text: "EN | FA"
- Users can switch language
- Google follows these links

**Example Switcher:**

```html
<div class="language-switcher">
  <a href="https://teznevisan3.com/" hreflang="fa">ÙØ§Ø±Ø³ÛŒ</a> |
  <a href="https://teznevisan3.com/en/" hreflang="en">English</a>
</div>
```


***

## ğŸ“ˆ **Why English Version HELPS SEO**

### **1. Captures English Search Traffic**

**New Queries You'll Rank For:**

```

"academic research Iran English"
```

**These don't compete with your Persian queries!**

### **2. Attracts Different Audience**

**English Version Targets:**

- International students studying IN Iran
- Iranian students abroad searching in English
- English-speaking academics needing Iran-based services
- Universities looking for Iran partnerships

**All NEW traffic, not cannibalizing Persian traffic**

### **3. Domain Authority Boost**

**English content gets backlinks from:**

- International student forums
- English academic sites
- Study abroad websites
- International directories

**These backlinks boost YOUR ENTIRE DOMAIN**, including Persian pages!

### **4. Better for AI Systems**

**AI Benefits:**

- ChatGPT can recommend you to English speakers

- Google AI Overview shows you for multilingual searches

**Your llms.txt becomes more valuable** with both languages!

## **PHASE 5: ON-PAGE SEO OPTIMIZATION** ğŸ”

### **Week 3-4: Optimize All Pages**

#### **A. All Service Pages (Persian \& English)**

- [ ] **Update Title Pattern**: `[Service] | Official Teznevisan | Since 2013`

- [ ] **Schema markup**: Service schema on each page

**Example Service Schema:**

```html
<script type="application/ld+json">
{
  "@context": "https://schema.org",
  "@type": "Service",
  "serviceType": "Master's Thesis Writing",
  "provider": {
    "@type": "Organization",
    "name": "Teznevisan Institute",
    "url": "https://teznevisan3.com"
  },
  "areaServed": {
    "@type": "Country",
    "name": "Iran"
  },
  "description": "Professional master's thesis writing service with 97% success rate"
}
</script>
```

    - Contact page (multiple places)

    - Related services
- [ ] **From Blog Posts** link to:
    - Relevant service pages
    - Official verification when mentioning brand
    - Contact page in CTAs
- [ ] **Cross-language linking**:
    - Persian pages â†’ English equivalents (language switcher)
    - English pages â†’ Persian equivalents (language switcher)


#### **C. Image Optimization**

- [ ] **Create official badges/seals**:
    - "Official Since 2013" badge (PNG/SVG)
    - "Iran's \#1" badge
    - "Verified Official Website" seal
- [ ] **Optimize all images**:
    - Compress (use TinyPNG or ShortPixel plugin)
    - Add descriptive filenames: `teznevisan-official-logo.png`
    - Add ALT text: `Official Teznevisan Institute logo - Since 2013`
    - Add title attributes
- [ ] **Add badges to**:
    - Homepage header
    - All service pages sidebar
    - Footer
    - Contact page


#### **D. URL Structure Audit**

**Persian Pages:**

- [ ] Clean URLs (no dates, no extra parameters)
- [ ] Include keyword when possible
- [ ] Not too long (<60 characters)

**English Pages:**

- [ ] All under /en/ subfolder
- [ ] Mirror Persian structure
- [ ] Clean, keyword-rich URLs

**Examples:**

```
âœ… GOOD:
teznevisan3.com/official-teznevisan-website/
teznevisan3.com/en/official-website/
teznevisan3.com/services/master-thesis/
teznevisan3.com/en/services/master-thesis/

âŒ BAD:
teznevisan3.com/2026/02/16/post-title/
teznevisan3.com/page-id-123/
teznevisan3.com/en-official-website/ (missing /en/ folder)
```


#### **E. Meta Tags Checklist (Every Page)**

- [ ] **Title tag**: 50-60 characters, includes "Official" or "Since 2013"
- [ ] **Meta description**: 150-160 characters, compelling, includes contact
- [ ] **Keywords meta** (optional): 5-10 relevant keywords
- [ ] **OG tags** (Open Graph for social sharing):

```html
<meta property="og:title" content="..." />
<meta property="og:description" content="..." />
<meta property="og:image" content="..." />
<meta property="og:url" content="..." />
```

- [ ] **Twitter Card tags**:

```html
<meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image" />
<meta name="twitter:title" content="..." />
<meta name="twitter:description" content="..." />
```


#### **F. Heading Structure (Every Page)**

- [ ] **One H1 per page** (main title)
- [ ] **H2s for main sections** (3-5 per page)
- [ ] **H3s for subsections** (as needed)
- [ ] **Logical hierarchy**: H1 > H2 > H3 (don't skip levels)
- [ ] **Include keywords** in headings naturally
- [ ] **Persian pages**: RTL-friendly headings
- [ ] **English pages**: LTR headings
