## **PHASE 6: TECHNICAL SEO** âš™ï¸

### **Week 4: Technical Optimization**

#### **A. Page Speed Optimization**

- [ ] **Install Caching Plugin**:
    - Option 1: WP Rocket (premium, \$49/year) - BEST
    - Option 2: W3 Total Cache (free)
    - Option 3: WP Super Cache (free)
- [ ] **Enable Caching**:
    - Page cache: ON
    - Browser cache: ON
    - Object cache: ON
    - Database cache: ON
- [ ] **Image Optimization**:
    - Install ShortPixel or Smush plugin
    - Compress existing images
    - Enable lazy loading
    - Convert to WebP format (ShortPixel does this)
- [ ] **Minify CSS/JS**:
    - Enable in caching plugin
    - Combine CSS files
    - Combine JS files
    - Remove unused CSS/JS
- [ ] **CDN Setup** (optional but recommended):
    - Cloudflare (free plan available)
    - Connect domain to Cloudflare
    - Enable caching rules
    - Enable auto minify
- [ ] **Database Optimization**:
    - Install WP-Optimize plugin
    - Clean post revisions
    - Clean spam comments
    - Clean transients
    - Optimize database tables
    - Schedule weekly auto-clean
- [ ] **Test Page Speed**:
    - Google PageSpeed Insights: https://pagespeed.web.dev/
    - GTmetrix: https://gtmetrix.com/
    - Target: 80+ score on mobile, 90+ on desktop


#### **B. Mobile Optimization**

- [ ] **Test Mobile Responsiveness**:
    - Google Mobile-Friendly Test
    - Test on actual mobile devices
    - Test language switcher on mobile
    - Test all CTAs clickable on mobile
- [ ] **Mobile-Specific Fixes**:
    - Ensure text readable without zooming (16px minimum)
    - Tap targets at least 48x48 pixels
    - No horizontal scrolling
    - Fast loading on 3G/4G
- [ ] **Viewport Meta Tag** (should already be there):

```html
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
```


#### **C. SSL/HTTPS**

- [ ] **Verify SSL Certificate** active
- [ ] **Force HTTPS** in WordPress:
    - Settings â†’ General
    - WordPress Address \& Site Address: https://
    - Save
- [ ] **Add HTTPS Redirect** in .htaccess:

```apache
RewriteEngine On
RewriteCond %{HTTPS} off
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}%{REQUEST_URI} [L,R=301]
```

- [ ] **Update all internal links** to https://
- [ ] **Check for mixed content** (http resources on https pages)


#### **D. XML Sitemap Configuration**

- [ ] **Yoast SEO â†’ General â†’ Features â†’ XML Sitemaps: ON**
- [ ] **Configure Sitemap Settings**:
    - Yoast SEO â†’ Search Appearance â†’ Content Types
    - Posts: Include in sitemap YES
    - Pages: Include in sitemap YES
    - Media: Include in sitemap NO
- [ ] **Verify Sitemaps Generated**:
    - Visit: teznevisan3.com/sitemap_index.xml
    - Should show multiple sitemaps (pages, posts, languages)
    - Click each to verify pages listed
- [ ] **Submit to Search Engines** (if not done):
    - Google Search Console
    - Bing Webmaster Tools


#### **E. Structured Data (Schema.org)**

**Add these schemas to relevant pages:**

- [ ] **Homepage**: Organization + WebSite + FAQPage schemas
- [ ] **About page**: Organization schema
- [ ] **Contact page**: LocalBusiness schema
- [ ] **Service pages**: Service schema for each
- [ ] **FAQ pages**: FAQPage schema with all Q\&As
- [ ] **Maziyar page**: Person schema
- [ ] **Blog posts**: Article schema

**Test Schemas**:

- [ ] Google Rich Results Test: https://search.google.com/test/rich-results
- [ ] Paste URL of each page
- [ ] Fix any errors/warnings


#### **F. Core Web Vitals**

- [ ] **Check in Google Search Console**:
    - Experience â†’ Core Web Vitals
    - Check mobile and desktop reports
- [ ] **Optimize LCP (Largest Contentful Paint)**:
    - Target: < 2.5 seconds
    - Optimize images above fold
    - Remove render-blocking resources
    - Use caching
- [ ] **Optimize FID (First Input Delay)**:
    - Target: < 100 milliseconds
    - Minimize JavaScript
    - Break up long tasks
- [ ] **Optimize CLS (Cumulative Layout Shift)**:
    - Target: < 0.1
    - Set image dimensions (width/height)
    - Reserve space for ads/embeds
    - Avoid inserting content above existing content

## **ğŸ“ IMPLEMENTATION NOTES**

### **Translation Tips**

- **Don't auto-translate**: Use professional translator or AI + human review
- **Adapt, don't just translate**: English version should emphasize Maziyar, international students
- **Consistent terminology**: Create glossary of key terms in both languages
- **Cultural adaptation**: English version more direct, Persian can be more formal


### **Common Pitfalls to Avoid**

1. âŒ **Forgetting hreflang tags** â†’ Confuses Google about language versions
2. âŒ **Duplicate content same language** â†’ SEO penalty
3. âŒ **Inconsistent contact info** â†’ Confuses users and AI
4. âŒ **Slow page speed** â†’ Hurts rankings
5. âŒ **No mobile optimization** â†’ Loses mobile traffic
6. âŒ **Ignoring schema markup** â†’ Miss rich results
7. âŒ **Not submitting to AI systems** â†’ Slow discovery
8. âŒ **Neglecting Persian while building English** â†’ Lose core market
9. âŒ **Over-optimizing** â†’ Sounds unnatural, AI detects
10. âŒ **Not tracking metrics** â†’ Can't measure success

### **Budget Estimate**

| Item | Cost (USD) | Priority |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| WPML Plugin | \$39/year | High |
| Translation (10 pages) | \$300-500 | High |
| Premium Theme (if needed) | \$60 one-time | Medium |
| WP Rocket Caching | \$49/year | Medium |
| ShortPixel Images | \$10/month | Medium |
| Ahrefs/SEMrush (optional) | \$99/month | Low |
| **Total Year 1** | **~\$600-800** | - |

**Or DIY approach**: Use free plugins (Polylang, W3 Cache, Smush) + self-translate = **~\$100/year**
